33 In my point of view problems in programming I found in myself and others : 1. find out his/her areas of interest in programming. 2. Wrong selection of language/area according to his/her potential. 3. Frequently move learning from one language to another. 4. Less consistency and patience. 5. Trying to be master of all within a very short time. 5. Less practice to gather maximum expertise in a specific area. 6. Always in a hurry to build up a software and satisfy/showing himself/herself as a software developer. 7. Most of us doing different course on different programming languages but get less opportunity for project-based learning. 8. Less dedication to finalize his/her working project. 9. Searching google to find out the related code and coping it. 10. Finally not wanted to write write and write maximum code in spite of error/bug.
